The subject Internet and Online Community teaches us an all-encompassing vision of technology and the Internet. How it's future will look like and the mechanisms behind it. How it works and is a must-learn for students as their future will depend on it. The only thing to improve is the platforms taught on as it is a little broad and can be hard to comprehend for low-tech students not used to operate in these circumstances.
